<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buigzaam.html>buigzaam</a> (61526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boochsaem</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buigen.html>buigen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-zaam</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buigzaam.html>buigzaam</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buigzamer.html>buigzamer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">buigzaamst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bendable, flexible</li>
<li>compliant</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***buik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buik.html>buik</a> (2280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buuc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">būc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*būkaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buik.html>buik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buiken.html>buiken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikje.html>buikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>belly</li>
<li>paunch (referring euphemistically to a protrusive belly)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The lowest inner part of a ship's hull, where water accumulates.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buikdanseres.html>buikdanseres</a> (54888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably formed directly from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikdansen.html>buikdansen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-eres</i>, otherwise from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">buikdanser</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-es</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikdanseres.html>buikdanseres</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikdanseressen.html>buikdanseressen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikdanseres.html>buikdanseresje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">buikdanser</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>female belly dancer</li></ol>
